Notice

PRO : Profession
NUM : Number (from 1 to 3647 ; Numbers 262 and 2683 represent the same person : n. 2683 is not reproduced)
COU : Country (F = born in France, I = Italy, G = Germany, B = Belgium, N = Netherlands, S = Switzerland)
DAY : Day of birth
MON : Month of birth
YEA : Year of birth
H : Hour of birth ; Birthtime is converted to standard time, either for zone 0 (= GMT) or -1 (= CET)
MN : Minutes
SEC : Seconds
TZ : Time Zone at the place of birth and date of birth (0 or -1)
LAT : Latitude of Birth place
LON : Longitude of Birth place
COD : Abbreviated Code of Birth place indicating County of birth or the French "Département"
CITY : Name of Birth place
 

Professions

C = sport Champion (vol. 1)
S = Scientist (vol. 2)
M = Military man (vol. 3)
P = Painter (vol. 4)
M = Musician (vol. 4)
A = Actor (vol. 5)
PT = Politician (vol. 5)
W = Writer (vol. 6)
J = Journalist (vol. 6)
 

Index (vol. 2) :

Médecins (Physicians) : n. 1-2552
Scientifiques (Men of science) : n. 2553-3647
 

Repartition by countries (vol. 2)

France : 1702
Germany : 861
Italy : 547
Belgium : 366
Netherlands : 154
Switzerland : 17
